<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aentrēden</i>. ***aantrekken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aantrekken.html>aantrekken</a> (4053)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aentrecken</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to, on</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trekken.html>trekken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pull</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aantrekken.html>aantrekken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to attract, exert a pulling force (on an object) such as gravity
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:magneet.html>magneet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:trekt.html>trekt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> ijzerdeeltjes <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The magnet <b>attracts</b> all iron particles.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to attract, draw, <a href = vnd.unilang:allure.html>allure</a>, appeal (to someone)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tighten by pulling</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put on (e.g. clothing)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take heed, to take an interest in something, to let oneself be bothered by
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:trek.html>Trek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geschreeuw.html>geschreeuw</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>let yourself be bothered</b> by their shouting.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenval</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:val.html>val</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<ol><li>An act of aggression; assault, attack

<li>A sudden convulsion; attack, seizure</li></ol>

***aanvoer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanvoer.html>aanvoer</a> (39876)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanvoeren.html>aanvoeren</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voer.html>voer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">load</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p><span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanvreten.html>aanvreten</a> (110106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vreten.html>vreten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to eat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanwezigheid.html>aanwezigheid</a> (2954)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanwezig.html>aanwezig</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanwezigheid.html>aanwezigheid</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanwezigheden.html>aanwezigheden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanwezigheid.html>aanwezigheidje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>presence
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Benedicts <a href = vnd.unilang:reagens.html>reagens</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bekend.html>bekend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> Benedicts <a href = vnd.unilang:oplossing.html>oplossing</a> of Benedicts test) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:reagens.html>reagens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebruikt.html>gebruikt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> test <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aanwezigheid.html>aanwezigheid</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> monosachariden (<a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>zoals</a> glucose <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fructose.html>fructose</a>); <a href = vnd.unilang:sommige.html>sommige</a> disachariden <a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>zoals</a> maltose <a href = vnd.unilang:reageren.html>reageren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:positief.html>positief</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>Meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:algemeen.html>algemeen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> Benedict <a href = vnd.unilang:reagens.html>reagens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebruikt.html>gebruikt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aanwezigheid.html>aanwezigheid</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> aldehyden in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oplossing.html>oplossing</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tonen.html>tonen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Benedict's reagent (also known as Benedict's solution or Benedict's test) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a reagent that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used as a test for the <b>presence</b> of monosaccharides (such as glucose and <a href = vnd.unilang:fructose.html>fructose</a>); some disaccharides such as maltose also react positively. More generally, Benedict's solution <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used to determine the <b>presence</b> of aldehydes in a solution.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>attendance</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:aanwezigheid.html>aanwezigheid</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenwisen</i>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aensetten</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zetten.html>zetten</a></i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start, switch on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>Heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> radio <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aangezet.html>aangezet</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Have you already <b><a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a></b> the radio <b>on</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to urge, incite [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></i> <span>(object)</span></span>]
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spreker.html>spreker</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zette.html>zette</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></b> protest.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The speaker <b>called for</b> protests.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stick, catch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ergative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to intensify, to increase
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> wind <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zette.html>zette</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The wind <b>began to blow faster</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***aanzien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanzien.html>aanzien</a> (5645)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aensien</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">ansehn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">ansehen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">onsēn</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanzien.html>aanzien</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to watch, to view</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to view as, to take for, to mistake for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zag.html>zag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vos.html>vos</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>mistook</b> a fox for a dog.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aangezien.html>aangezien</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">aanzicht</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aensien</i>, equivalent to the <a href = vnd.unilang:gerund.html>gerund</a> of the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanzien.html>aanzien</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***aap.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aap.html>aap</a> (2105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">āpe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*apo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*apô</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aap.html>aap</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:apen.html>apen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aapje.html>aapje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">apin</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>monkey, ape, simian; any member of the infraorder Simiiformes</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aapje.html>aapje</a> (8775)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The carriage <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> named after the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:A.R.M." class="extiw" title="wikipedia:nl:A.R.M.">A.<a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>.M.</a> drivers' <a href = vnd.unilang:uniforms.html>uniforms</a>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> compared to those of the uniformed <a href = vnd.unilang:monkeys.html>monkeys</a> of street and <a href = vnd.unilang:circus.html>circus</a> artists.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aar.html>aar</a> (41162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">âer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ār</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ahaz</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">āer</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardappel.html>aardappel</a> (10523)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soil, earth, ground</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:appel.html>appel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">apple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> English <i>earthapple</i>; French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">pomme <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:terre.html>terre</a></i>, Luxembourgish <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">Gromper</i> (originally "ground pear"), German regionally both <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Erdapfel</i> ("earth apple") and <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Grundbirne</i> ("ground pear")
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardbei.html>aardbei</a> (17709)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">erdbere</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*erdberi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*erþōbazją</i>. Compare German <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">Erdbeere</i>, West Frisian <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">ierdbei</i>, Danish <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">jordbær</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarden.html>aarden</a> (52522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">erdijn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*irthīn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*irþīnaz</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>. Reformed by analogy with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarden.html>aarden</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>earthen, made of soil</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> etc., made of pottery made from soil</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarden.html>aarden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ground, connect an electrical conductor as a safety outlet</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to commit to the earth, bury
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begraven.html>begraven</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestellen.html>bestellen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aard.html>aard</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (<i>used with <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> ...)</i> to take after, share (notably inherited) traits with (notably an ancestor)</li></ol>

***aardkloot.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardkloot.html>aardkloot</a> (77575)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aard.html>aard</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">earth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kloot.html>kloot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lump, clod</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aardkloot.html>aardkloot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aardkloot.html>aardkloten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aardkloot.html>aardklootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated, poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Planet Earth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oneerlijk.html>oneerlijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardkloot.html>aardkloot</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">How unfair life <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> on this planet of ours!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> any (<a href = vnd.unilang:rocky.html>rocky</a>) planet</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:kloot.html>Kloot</a></i>, when used on its own, <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> developed into a vulgar synonym for <i><a href = vnd.unilang:testikel.html>testikel</a></i>, meaning <i>testicle</i> and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used as an expletive corresponding with <i>bollocks</i>. In the compound noun <i><a href = vnd.unilang:aardkloot.html>aardkloot</a></i>, however, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kloot.html>kloot</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> retained its original meaning of ‘lump of earth’ and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not usually considered offensive. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> restricted to literary or ironic <a href = vnd.unilang:registers.html>registers</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">planet earth</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">aardbol</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:blauwe.html>blauwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:planeet.html>planeet</a></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:aardkloot.html>aardkloot</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:verouderd.html>verouderd</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bolvormig.html>bolvormige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:planeet.html>planeet</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blauwe.html>blauwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:planeet.html>planeet</a>

***aardrijkskunde.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardrijkskunde.html>aardrijkskunde</a> (23602)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
